';} function selectVariant(v){selectedVariant=v;document.querySelectorAll('.variant-chip').forEach(function(el){el.classList.toggle('selected',el.textContent===v)});} function changeQty(d){qty=Math.max(1,qty+d);document.getElementById('qty-display').textContent=qty;} function addToCart(){if(!currentProd)return;if(currentProd.variants&¤tProd.variants.length>1&&!selectedVariant){toast2('Please select a variant');return;}var existing=cart.find(function(i){return i.id===currentProd.id&&i.variant===selectedVariant});if(existing)existing.qty+=qty;else cart.push({id:currentProd.id,name:currentProd.name,price:currentProd.price,img:currentProd.img,variant:selectedVariant,qty:qty});updateCartBadge();closeProdSheet();toast2(qty+'x '+currentProd.name+' added!');} function updateCartBadge(){var total=cart.reduce(function(s,i){return s+i.qty},0);document.getElementById('cart-count-badge').textContent=total;document.getElementById('cart-btn').style.display=total>0?'block':'none';} function openCart(){renderCartItems();document.getElementById('cart-overlay').classList.add('open');} function closeCart(){document.getElementById('cart-overlay').classList.remove('open');} function renderCartItems(){var el=document.getElementById('cart-items-list');var checkoutBtn=document.getElementById('checkout-btn');if(!cart.length){el.innerHTML='

('+i.variant+')':'')+' x'+i.qty+' — £'+(i.price*i.qty).toFixed(2)}).join(' ');var msg='🛍️ NEW ORDER — JRSHOP '+'━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━ '+'Order ID: '+orderId+' '+'👤 CUSTOMER '+'Name: '+name+' '+'Phone: '+phone+' '+(document.getElementById('co-email').value?'Email: '+document.getElementById('co-email').value+' ':'')+' 📦 ITEMS '+itemsList+' '+'💰 TOTAL: £'+total.toFixed(2)+' '+'📍 DELIVERY ADDRESS '+addr+', '+city+', '+post+', UK '+(document.getElementById('co-note').value?' 📝 Note: '+document.getElementById('co-note').value+' ':'')+' 📋 ORDER CODE (for tracking): '+orderId+' [Data:'+btoa(unescape(encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(orderData))))+']';var url=MESSENGER_LINK||'https://www.messenger.com';if(!url.startsWith('http'))url='https://'+url;window.open(url,'_blank');setTimeout(function(){navigator.clipboard.writeText(msg).catch(function(){});document.getElementById('checkout-overlay').classList.remove('open');showSuccess(orderId)},500);} function showSuccess(orderId){document.body.innerHTML+='
